<h1 _ngcontent-fha-c119="" class="doc-title ng-star-inserted" title="Swiper"> Swiper </h1>

<div _ngcontent-fha-c106="" auitextselectionexpansion="" class="markdown-body ng-star-inserted renderOptimization" style="position: relative;">   <div>    <p>滑块视图容器，提供子组件滑动轮播显示的能力。</p>    <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">      <ul>       <li>        <p>该组件从API version 7开始支持。后续版本如有新增内容，则采用上角标单独标记该内容的起始版本。</p></li>       <li>        <p>Swiper组件内包含了<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-gestures-pangesture">PanGesture</a>拖动手势事件，用于滑动轮播子组件。<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#disableswipe8">disableSwipe</a>属性设为true会取消内部的PanGesture事件监听。</p></li>       <li>        <p>Swiper中复用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-nodecontainer">NodeContainer</a>时，禁止递归流程中子节点更新父节点状态变量。</p></li>      </ul>     </div></div></div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 578px;">     <h2 id="子组件" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">子组件<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="子组件" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>可以包含子组件。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <ul>        <li>         <p>子组件类型：系统组件和自定义组件，支持渲染控制类型（<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-rendering-control-ifelse" target="_blank">if/else</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-rendering-control-foreach" target="_blank">ForEach</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-rendering-control-lazyforeach" target="_blank">LazyForEach</a>和<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-new-rendering-control-repeat" target="_blank">Repeat</a>）。不建议子组件中混用懒加载组件（包括LazyForEach、Repeat）和非懒加载组件，或者子组件中使用多个懒加载组件，否则可能导致懒加载组件预加载能力失效等问题。不建议在组件动画过程中对数据源进行操作，否则会导致布局出现异常。</p></li>        <li>         <p>Swiper子组件的<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-visibility#visibility">visibility</a>属性设置为Visibility.None，且Swiper的displayCount属性设置为'auto'时，对应子组件在视窗内不占位，但不影响导航点个数；visibility属性设置为Visibility.None或者Visibility.Hidden时，对应子组件不显示，但依然会在视窗内占位。</p></li>        <li>         <p>当Swiper子组件设置了<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-location#offset">offset</a>属性时，会按照子组件的层级进行绘制，层级高的子组件会覆盖层级低的子组件。例如，Swiper包含3个子组件，其中第3个子组件设置了offset({ x : 100 })，那么在横向循环滑动中，第3个子组件会覆盖第1个子组件，此时可设置第1个子组件的<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-z-order">zIndex</a>属性值大于第3个子组件，使第1个子组件层级高于第3个子组件。</p></li>        <li>         <p>在走焦到用户定义的子节点时，导航点、箭头会由于<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-common-events-focus-event#焦点样式" target="_blank">焦点样式</a>修改zIndex的行为被遮挡。</p></li>        <li>         <p>在包含大量子组件的场景中，建议采用懒加载、缓存数据、预加载数据和组件复用等方法，以优化Swiper的性能并减少内存占用。最佳实践请参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/best-practices/bpta-swiper_high_performance_development_guide" target="_blank">优化Swiper组件加载慢丢帧问题</a>。</p></li>       </ul>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 573px;">     <h2 id="接口" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">接口<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="接口" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>Swiper(controller?: SwiperController)</p>     <p>创建滑块视图容器。</p>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 10开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">controller</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#swipercontroller">SwiperController</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">给组件绑定一个控制器，用来控制组件翻页或者预加载指定子节点。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 274px;">     <h2 id="属性" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">属性<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="属性" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>除支持<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-component-general-attributes">通用属性</a>外，还支持以下属性：</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>Swiper组件<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-sharp-clipping">通用属性clip</a>的默认值为true。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 669px;">     <h3 id="index" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">index<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="index" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>index(value: number)</p>     <p>设置当前在容器中显示的子组件的索引值。设置小于0或大于等于子组件数量时，按照默认值0处理。</p>     <p>从API version 10开始，该属性支持<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-two-way-sync" target="_blank">$$</a>双向绑定变量。</p>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 10开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>当前在容器中显示的子组件的索引值。</p>          <p>默认值：0</p>          <p><strong>说明：</strong></p>          <p>设置的值小于0或大于最大页面索引时，取0。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 613px;">     <h3 id="autoplay" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">autoPlay<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="autoplay" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>autoPlay(value: boolean)</p>     <p>设置子组件是否自动播放。轮播方向为索引从小到大。</p>     <p><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#loop">loop</a>为false时，自动轮播到最后一页时停止轮播。手势切换后不是最后一页时继续播放。当Swiper不可见时会停止轮播。</p>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 10开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>子组件是否自动播放。</p>          <p>默认值：false，不自动轮播。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 874px;">     <h3 id="autoplay18" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">autoPlay<sup>18+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="autoplay18" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>autoPlay(autoPlay: boolean, options: AutoPlayOptions)</p>     <p>设置子组件是否自动播放。options入参控制手指或者鼠标等按下屏幕时子组件是否停止自动播放。</p>     <p>当<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#loop">loop</a>设置为false时，自动轮播将在到达最后一页时停止。在通过手势切换且未处于最后一页的情况下，轮播将继续进行。Swiper在不可见时，轮播也将停止。</p>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 18开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 18开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">autoPlay</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>子组件是否自动播放。</p>          <p>默认值：false，不自动轮播。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">options</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#autoplayoptions18对象说明">AutoPlayOptions</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>配置手指或者鼠标等按下屏幕时子组件是否停止自动播放。当stopWhenTouched设置为true时，多指按下场景中任意一个手指抬起后，将自动继续播放。</p>          <p>默认值：{ stopWhenTouched: true }，停止自动播放。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 733px;">     <h3 id="indicator" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">indicator<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="indicator" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>indicator(value: DotIndicator | DigitIndicator | boolean)</p>     <p>设置可选导航点指示器样式。</p>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 10开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.9.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.9.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.9.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.9.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#dotindicator10">DotIndicator</a><sup>10+</sup> | <a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#digitindicator10">DigitIndicator</a><sup>10+</sup> | boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>可选导航点指示器样式。</p>          <p>- DotIndicator：圆点指示器样式。</p>          <p>- DigitIndicator：数字指示器样式。</p>          <p>- boolean：是否启用导航点指示器。设置为true启用，false不启用。</p>          <p>默认值：true</p>          <p>默认类型：DotIndicator</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1041px;">     <h3 id="indicator15" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">indicator<sup>15+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="indicator15" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>indicator(indicator: IndicatorComponentController | DotIndicator | DigitIndicator | boolean)</p>     <p>设置外部绑定的导航点组件控制器。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>设置外部绑定的导航点组件控制器后，可以和外部导航点结合使用。外部导航点支持自定义设置显示位置和大小。详细介绍可参看<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-swiper-components-indicator">Indicator</a>。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 15开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 15开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">indicator</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-swiper-components-indicator#indicatorcomponentcontroller">IndicatorComponentController</a><sup>15+</sup> | <a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#dotindicator10">DotIndicator</a> | <a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#digitindicator10">DigitIndicator</a> | boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>可选导航点指示器样式。</p>          <p>- IndicatorComponentController：单独导航点指示器控制器。当使用单独导航点指示器控制器时，可以与外部单独导航点进行绑定，但是绑定的单独导航点和内置导航点不能同时存在。</p>          <p>- DotIndicator：圆点指示器样式。</p>          <p>- DigitIndicator：数字指示器样式。</p>          <p>- boolean：是否启用导航点指示器。设置为true启用，false不启用。</p>          <p>默认值：true</p>          <p>默认类型：DotIndicator。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 565px;">     <h3 id="loop"  <p>默认值：true</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 565px;">     <h3 id="effectmode8" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">duration<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="duration" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>duration(value: number)</p>     <p>设置子组件切换的动画时长。</p>     <p>duration需要和<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#curve8">curve</a>一起使用。</p>     <p>curve默认曲线为<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-curve#curvesinterpolatingspring10">interpolatingSpring</a>，此时动画时长只受曲线自身参数影响，不再受duration的控制。不受duration控制的曲线可以查阅<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-curve">插值计算</a>模块，比如，<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-curve#curvesspringmotion9">springMotion</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-curve#curvesresponsivespringmotion9">responsiveSpringMotion</a>和interpolatingSpring类型的曲线不受duration控制。如果希望动画时长受到duration控制，需要给curve设置其他曲线。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder"> class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 685px;">     <h3 id="itemspace" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">itemSpace<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="itemspace" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>itemSpace(value: number | string)</p>     <p>设置子组件与子组件之间间隙。不支持设置百分比。</p>     <p>类型为number时，默认单位vp。类型为string时，需要显式指定像素单位，如'10px'；未指定像素单位时，如'10'，单位为vp。</p>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 10开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.17.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.17.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.17.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.17.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number | string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>子组件与子组件之间间隙。</p>          <p>默认值：0</p>          <p>取值范围：[0, +∞)，当设置数值小于0或超出Swiper组件宽度范围时，按照默认值处理。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 841px;">     <h3 id="cachedcount8" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">cachedCount<sup>8+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="cachedcount8" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>cachedCount(value: number)</p>     <p>设置预加载子组件个数，以当前页面为基准，加载当前显示页面的前后个数。前面item删除，后面会向前补位。例如cachedCount=1时，会将当前显示的页面的前面一页和后面一页的子组件都预加载。如果设置为按组翻页，即displayCount的swipeByGroup参数设为true，预加载时会以组为基本单位。例如cachedCount=1，swipeByGroup=true时，会将当前组的前面一组和后面一组的子组件都预加载。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <ul>        <li>         <p>在连续滑动场景中，一屏显示一个Swiper子组件时，通常将cachedCount值设置为1或2即可。最佳实践请参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/best-practices/bpta-swiper_high_performance_development_guide#section143504547145" target="_blank">优化Swiper组件加载慢丢帧问题-缓存数据项</a>。</p></li>        <li>         <p>只在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-rendering-control-lazyforeach" target="_blank">LazyForEach</a>和开启了virtualScroll开关的<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-new-rendering-control-repeat" target="_blank">Repeat</a>中生效，生效后超出显示及缓存范围的子节点会被释放。</p></li>       </ul>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 10开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.18.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.18.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left"   <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 854px;">     <h3 id="cachedcount15" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">cachedCount<sup>15+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="cachedcount15" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>cachedCount(count: number, isShown: boolean)</p>     <p>设置预加载子组件个数。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <ul>        <li>isShown属性为true，且设置的count过大时，如果前后预加载范围内可加载的节点不足，循环场景下同一个可加载节点只会布局在一侧。</li>       </ul>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 15开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 15开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.19.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.19.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left"   <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">count</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>预加载子组件个数。</p>          <p>默认值：1</p>          <p>取值范围：[0, +∞)，设置小于0的值时，按照默认值处理。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">isShown</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>预加载范围内的节点是否进行绘制，不下渲染树。</p>          <p>默认值：false，预加载范围内的节点不进行绘制。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 589px;">     <h3 id="disableswipe8" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">disableSwipe<sup>8+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="disableswipe8" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>disableSwipe(value: boolean)</p>     <p>设置禁用组件滑动切换功能。</p>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 10开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.20.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.20.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.20.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.20.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>禁用组件滑动切换功能。设置为true禁用，false不禁用。</p>          <p>默认值：false</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 2642px;">     <h3 id="displaycount8" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">displayCount<sup>8+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="displaycount8" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>displayCount(value: number | string | SwiperAutoFill, swipeByGroup?: boolean)</p>     <p>设置Swiper视窗内元素显示个数。</p>     <p>使用number类型时，子元素主轴宽度会基于Swiper主轴宽度适应。子组件按照主轴均分Swiper宽度（减去displayCount-1个itemSpace）的方式进行主轴拉伸（收缩）布局，设置为小于等于0的值时，按默认值1显示。</p>     <p>使用string类型时，根据子元素的主轴宽度线性布局，不再适应Swiper主轴宽度。此时value值仅支持设置为'auto'，设置<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#customcontenttransition12">customContentTransition</a>和<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#oncontentdidscroll12">onContentDidScroll</a>事件不生效。</p>     <p>使用SwiperAutoFill类型时，子元素主轴宽度会基于Swiper主轴宽度适应。通过设置一个子组件最小宽度值minSize，会根据Swiper当前宽度和minSize值自动计算并更改一页内元素显示个数。当minSize为空或者小于等于0时，Swiper显示1列。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <ul>        <li>         <p>按组进行翻页时，判定翻页的拖拽距离阈值将调整为Swiper宽度的50%（若按子元素翻页，该阈值为子元素宽度的50%）。若最后一组的子元素数量少于displayCount，将利用占位子元素进行填充，占位子元素仅用于布局定位，不显示任何内容，其位置将直接显示Swiper的背景样式。</p></li>        <li>         <p>displayCount设置为'auto'，并且设置非循环时，选中导航点的位置与视窗内首个页面的位置保持一致。如果翻页完成后，视窗内首个页面仅部分显示在视窗内，选中导航点亦与页面的位置保持一致，位于两个未选中的导航点之间。在此情况下，建议开发者隐藏导航点。</p></li>        <li>         <p>导航点样式设定为圆形导航点，视窗内显示子元素数量等于1时（单页场景）或者 displayCount设置为'auto'时，显示导航点数量等于子元素数量。</p></li>        <li>         <p>displayCount设置为'auto'时，若设置swipeByGroup为true，则单个子元素按组翻页，一次只能翻一页。在此情况下，建议开发者不设置swipeByGroup或者设置swipeByGroup为false。</p></li>        <li>         <p>从API version 18开始，该接口支持在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-attribute-modifier#attributemodifier">attributeModifier</a>中调用。</p></li>       </ul>      </div></div></div>     <p>当导航点样式设定为圆形导航点，视窗内显示子元素数量大于1（多页场景），显示导航点数量情况如下表：</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.21.9.1.6.1.1" width="20%">子元素总数量是否大于视窗内显示的子元素数量</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.21.9.1.6.1.2" width="20%">是否按组翻页</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.21.9.1.6.1.3" width="20%">是否循环</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.21.9.1.6.1.4" width="20%">圆形导航点显示数量</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.21.9.1.6.1.5" width="20%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">loop设置为true</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">圆形导航点的数量将与组数相等（组数计算方式为子元素总数量除以视窗内显示的子元素数量，若除不尽，则向上取整）</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">该效果在displayCount设置为'auto'时不生效</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">loop设置为false</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">圆形导航点的数量将与组数相等（组数计算方式为子元素总数量除以视窗内显示的子元素数量，若除不尽，则向上取整）</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">该效果在displayCount设置为'auto'时不生效</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">loop设置为true</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">圆形导航点的数量将与实际可翻页次数一致（显示导航点的数量等于子元素总数量）</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">——</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">loop设置为false</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">圆形导航点的数量将与实际可翻页次数一致（计算方式是子元素的总数量减去视窗内显示的子元素数量+1个）</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">该效果在displayCount设置为'auto'时不生效</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否（同时子元素的总数量大于0）</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">——</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">——</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">显示1个圆形导航点</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">该效果在displayCount设置为'auto'时不生效</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否（同时子元素的总数量等于0）</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">——</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">——</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">显示0个圆形导航点</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">——</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 10开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.21.14.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.21.14.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.21.14.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.21.14.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number | string | <a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#swiperautofill10">SwiperAutoFill</a><sup>10+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>视窗内显示的子元素个数。</p>          <p>默认值：1</p>          <p>取值范围：(0, +∞)，设置小于等于0的值时，按照默认值处理。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">swipeByGroup<sup>11+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>是否按组进行翻页。如果设为true，在翻页时会按组进行翻页，每组内子元素的数量为displayCount value的值；如果为false，则为默认翻页行为，即按照子元素进行翻页。</p>          <p>默认值：false</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>当Swiper子组件个数小于等于Swiper组件内容区内显示的节点总个数(totalDisplayCount = DisplayCount + prevMargin? (1 : 0) + nextMargin? (1 : 0))时，一般按照非循环模式布局处理，此时，前后边距对应子组件不显示，但依然会在视窗内占位。Swiper组件按照totalDisplayCount个数判断测算规格。例外情况如下：</p>       <ul>        <li>         <p>当Swiper子组件个数等于Swiper组件内容区内显示的节点总个数且prevMargin和nextMargin都生效时，设置loop为true支持循环。</p></li>        <li>         <p>当Swiper子组件个数等于Swiper组件DisplayCount数 + 1，且prevMargin和nextMargin至少一个生效时，在非按组翻页模式下设置loop为true，会生成截图占位组件(如果使用图片异步加载等显示耗时较长的组件可能不能正确生成截图，不建议在该场景开启循环)，支持循环。</p></li>       </ul>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1038px;">     <h3 id="displayarrow10" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">displayArrow<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="displayarrow10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>displayArrow(value: ArrowStyle | boolean, isHoverShow?: boolean)</p>     <p>设置导航点箭头样式。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>Swiper视窗内显示所有子节点时，只显示一屏，无法翻页，左右翻页箭头均不显示。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.22.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.22.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.22.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.22.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#arrowstyle10对象说明">ArrowStyle</a> | boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>支持设置箭头和底板样式，异常场景使用ArrowStyle对象中的默认值。设置为false不显示箭头和底板，true显示默认的箭头和底板样式。</p>          <p>默认值：false</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">isHoverShow</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>设置鼠标悬停时是否显示箭头。</p>          <p>默认值：false</p>          <p><strong>说明：</strong></p>          <p>1. isHoverShow为false时，常驻显示箭头。</p>          <p>2. isHoverShow为true时，有导航点时鼠标悬停在导航点和箭头范围内显示箭头，无导航点时鼠标悬停在Swiper显示范围内显示箭头。</p>          <p>3. 箭头显示时，支持点击翻页。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 613px;">     <h3 id="displaymode" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">displayMode<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="displaymode" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>displayMode(value: SwiperDisplayMode)</p>     <p>设置主轴方向上元素排列的模式，优先以<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#displaycount8">displayCount</a>设置的个数显示，displayCount未设置时本属性生效。</p>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 10开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.23.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.23.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.23.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.23.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#swiperdisplaymode枚举说明">SwiperDisplayMode</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>主轴方向上元素排列的模式。</p>          <p>默认值：SwiperDisplayMode.STRETCH</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1182px;">     <h3 id="nextmargin10" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">nextMargin<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="nextmargin10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>nextMargin(value: Length, ignoreBlank?:boolean)</p>     <p>设置后边距，用于露出后一项的一小部分，使用效果可以参考<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#示例1设置导航点交互及翻页动效">示例1设置导航点交互及翻页动效</a>。仅当Swiper子组件的布局方式为拉伸时生效，主要包括两种场景：1、displayMode属性设置为SwiperDisplayMode.STRETCH；2、displayCount属性设置为number类型。</p>     <p>当主轴方向为横向布局时，nextMargin或prevMargin中任意一个大于子组件测算的宽度，nextMargin和prevMargin均不显示。</p>     <p>当主轴方向为纵向布局时，nextMargin或prevMargin中任意一个大于子组件测算的高度，nextMargin和prevMargin均不显示。</p>     <p>使用nextMargin/prevMargin接口时，不要对子组件进行<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-size#constraintsize">尺寸范围限制</a>，否则子节点主轴将不会被拉伸到预期长度，边距失去效果。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>该接口不支持在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-attribute-modifier#attributemodifier">attributeModifier</a>中调用。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.24.11.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.24.11.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.24.11.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.24.11.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#length">Length</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>后边距。不支持设置百分比。</p>          <p>默认值：0</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">ignoreBlank<sup>12+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>非loop场景下尾页不显示nextMargin。在非loop场景下，设置为true时，尾页不显示空白的nextMargin，尾页的右边缘与Swiper视窗右边缘对齐；设置false时，尾页显示空白nextMargin，尾页的右边缘与Swiper视窗右边缘的距离为nextMargin。</p>          <p>默认值：false</p>          <p><strong>说明：</strong></p>          <p>尾页场景下，prevMargin和nextMargin的值相加作为左边边距显示前一个页面。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1182px;">     <h3 id="prevmargin10" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">prevMargin<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.25.11.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 705px;">     <h3 id="nestedscroll11" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">nestedScroll<sup>11+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="nestedscroll11" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>nestedScroll(value: SwiperNestedScrollMode)</p>     <p>设置Swiper组件和父组件的嵌套滚动模式。loop为true时Swiper组件没有边缘，不会触发父组件嵌套滚动。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.26.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.26.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.26.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.26.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#swipernestedscrollmode11枚举说明">SwiperNestedScrollMode</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>Swiper组件和父组件的嵌套滚动模式。</p>          <p>默认值：SwiperNestedScrollMode.SELF_ONLY</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>由于Swiper的抛滑动画逻辑和其它滚动类组件不同（Swiper一次只能滑动一页，抛滑时做翻页动画），当Swiper内嵌套其它滚动组件时，如果Swiper的翻页动画已经启动，将无法接受子节点上传的滚动偏移量。这时Swiper的翻页动画和子节点的边缘效果动画会同时执行。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 541px;">     <h3 id="indicatorinteractive12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">indicatorInteractive<sup>12+</sup><i style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 589px;">     <h3 id="pageflipmode15" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">pageFlipMode<sup>15+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 877px;">     <h3 id="maintainvisiblecontentposition20" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">maintainVisibleContentPosition<sup>20+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="maintainvisiblecontentposition20" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>maintainVisibleContentPosition(enabled: boolean)</p>     <p>设置显示区域上方或前方插入或删除数据时是否保持可见内容位置不变。适用于使用单一<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-rendering-control-lazyforeach" target="_blank">LazyForEach</a>作为Swiper子节点的情况，通过LazyForEach的<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-rendering-control-lazyforeach#ondataadd8">onDateAdd</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-rendering-control-lazyforeach#ondatadelete8">onDataDelete</a>等接口修改数据源。其他场景下，显示区域上方或前方插入或删除数据，可见内容位置会变化。</p>     <p>在<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#displaycount8">displayCount</a>属性的swipeByGroup参数设置为true，生效按组翻页时，一次在显示区域上方或前方插入或删除和一组节点数量倍数的数据量时才能保持可见内容位置不变，否则可见内容位置可能会随每组数据重新分组改变。</p>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 20开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 20开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.29.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.29.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.29.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.29.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">enabled</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>设置显示区域上方或前方插入或删除数据时是否要保持可见内容位置不变。</p>          <p>默认值：false，显示区域上方或前方插入或删除数据时可见内容位置会跟随变化。 true：显示区域上方或前方插入或删除数据时可见内容位置不变。如果改变数据源是在动画过程中，由于目标索引变化会导致动画停止。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 2256px;">     <h2 id="indicatorstyledeprecated对象说明" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">IndicatorStyle<sup>(deprecated)</sup>对象说明<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="indicatorstyledeprecated对象说明" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>从API version 8开始支持，从API version 10开始不再维护，建议使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#indicator10">indicator</a>代替。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.30.4.1.6.1.1" width="20%">名称</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.30.4.1.6.1.2" width="20%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.30.4.1.6.1.3" width="20%">只读</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.30.4.1.6.1.4" width="20%">可选</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.30.4.1.6.1.5" width="20%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">left</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#length">Length</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>设置导航点左侧相对于Swiper的位置。</p>          <p>未设置left和right时，进行自适应大小布局，按照指示器本身大小和Swiper的大小在主轴方向上进行居中对齐</p>          <p>设置为0时：按照0位置布局计算</p>          <p>优先级：高于right属性</p>          <p>取值范围：[0,Swiper宽度-导航点区域宽度]，超出该范围时，取最近的边界值。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">top</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#length">Length</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>设置导航点顶部相对于Swiper的位置。</p>          <p>未设置top和bottom时，进行自适应大小布局，按照指示器本身大小和Swiper的大小，在交叉轴方向上，位于底部，效果与设置bottom=0一致</p>          <p>设置为0时：按照0位置布局计算</p>          <p>优先级：高于bottom属性</p>          <p>取值范围：[0,Swiper高度-导航点区域高度]，超出该范围时，取最近的边界值。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">right</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#length">Length</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>设置导航点右侧相对于Swiper的位置。</p>          <p>未设置left和right时，进行自适应大小布局，按照指示器本身大小和Swiper的大小在主轴方向上进行居中对齐</p>          <p>设置为0时：按照0位置布局计算</p>          <p>优先级：低于left属性</p>          <p>取值范围：[0,Swiper宽度-导航点区域宽度]，超出该范围时，取最近的边界值。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">bottom</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#length">Length</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>设置导航点底部相对于Swiper的位置。</p>          <p>未设置top和bottom时，进行自适应大小布局，按照指示器本身大小和Swiper的大小，在交叉轴方向上，位于底部，效果与设置bottom=0一致</p>          <p>设置为0时：按照0位置布局计算</p>          <p>优先级：低于top属性</p>          <p>取值范围：[0,Swiper高度-导航点区域高度]，超出该范围时，取最近的边界值。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">size</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#length">Length</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>设置导航点的直径，不支持设置百分比。</p>          <p>默认值：6vp</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">mask</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>设置是否显示导航点蒙层样式。</p>          <p>设置为true时显示导航点蒙层样式，为false时不显示。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">color</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#resourcecolor">ResourceColor</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">设置导航点的颜色。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">selectedColor</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#resourcecolor">ResourceColor</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">设置选中的导航点的颜色。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1022px;">     <h2 id="swiperdisplaymode枚举说明" 7开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">AutoLinear<sup>(deprecated)</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">          <p>Swiper滑动一页的宽度为子组件宽度中的最大值。此枚举表现形式与<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#displaycount8">displayCount</a>中使用string类型，将值设置为auto表现一致，具体可参考<a 7开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">STRETCH<sup>10+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">          <p>Swiper滑动一页的宽度为Swiper组件自身的宽度。</p>          <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 10开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">AUTO_LINEAR<sup>(deprecated)</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">          <p>Swiper滑动一页的宽度为视窗内最左侧子组件的宽度。此枚举表现形式与<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#displaycount8">displayCount</a>中使用string类型，将值设置为auto表现一致，具体可参考<a 10开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div id="showprevious" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">showPrevious<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon id="changeindex12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">changeIndex<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.37.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.37.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.37.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder"    <p>设置的值小于0或大于最大页面索引时，取0。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">useAnimation</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1062px;">     <h3 id="changeindex15" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">changeIndex<sup>15+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="changeindex15" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>changeIndex(index: number, animationMode?: SwiperAnimationMode | boolean)</p>     <p>翻页至指定页面。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>该接口本身提供了不带动画跳转页面的能力（animationMode设置为false或者SwiperAnimationMode.NO_ANIMATION），不建议使用changeIndex接口启动动画后，直接使用finishAnimation接口打断来实现页面不带动画跳转。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 15开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 15开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.38.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.38.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.38.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.38.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">index</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>指定页面在Swiper中的索引值。</p>          <p><strong>说明：</strong></p>          <p>设置的值小于0或大于最大页面索引时，取0。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">animationMode</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#swiperanimationmode15枚举说明">SwiperAnimationMode</a> | boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>设置翻页至指定页面时的动效模式。</p>          <p>默认值：SwiperAnimationMode.NO_ANIMATION</p>          <p><strong>说明：</strong></p>          <p>当传入true时有动效，等同于SwiperAnimationMode.DEFAULT_ANIMATION；当传入false时无动效，等同于SwiperAnimationMode.NO_ANIMATION。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 517px;">     <h3 id="finishanimation" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">finishAnimation<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="finishanimation" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>finishAnimation(callback?: VoidCallback)</p>     <p>停止播放动画。</p>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 10开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.39.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.39.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.39.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.39.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">callback</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#voidcallback12">VoidCallback</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">动画结束的回调。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1270px;">     <h3 id="preloaditems18" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">preloadItems<sup>18+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="preloaditems18" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>preloadItems(indices: Optional&lt;Array&lt;number&gt;&gt;): Promise&lt;void&gt;</p>     <p>控制Swiper预加载指定子节点。调用该接口后会一次性加载所有指定的子节点，因此为了性能考虑，建议分批加载子节点。</p>     <p>如果SwiperController对象未绑定任何Swiper组件，直接调用该接口，会抛出JS异常，并返回错误码100004。因此使用该接口时，建议通过try-catch捕获异常。</p>     <p>与<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-rendering-control-lazyforeach" target="_blank">LazyForEach</a>和自定义组件结合使用时，由于<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-rendering-control-lazyforeach" target="_blank">LazyForEach</a>只会保留缓存范围内的自定义组件，在缓存范围外的会被删除，因此需要开发者保证通过该接口预加载的节点index在缓存范围内。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>Swiper的preloadItems需要在Swiper创建之后去调用，首次预加载推荐在Swiper的<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-events-show-hide#onappear">onAppear</a>生命周期中去控制。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 18开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 18开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.40.11.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.40.11.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.40.11.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.40.11.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">indices</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Optional&lt;Array&lt;number&gt;&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">需预加载的子节点的下标数组。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.40.13.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.40.13.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Promise&lt;void&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">预加载完成后触发的回调。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-universal">通用错误码</a>和<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-scroll">滚动类组件错误码</a>错误码。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.40.16.1.3.1.1" width="50%">错误码ID</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.40.16.1.3.1.2" width="50%">错误信息</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">401</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Parameter invalid. Possible causes: 1. The parameter type is not Array&lt;number&gt;; 2. The parameter is an empty array; 3. The parameter contains an invalid index.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">100004</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Controller not bound to component.</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 543px;">     <h2 id="swiperanimationmode15枚举说明" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">SwiperAnimationMode<sup>15+</sup>枚举说明<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>Swiper组件翻页至指定页面的动效模式。</p>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 15开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 15开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th    <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">NO_ANIMATION</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">0</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" 326px;">     <h2 id="indicator10" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">Indicator<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="indicator10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>设置导航点距离Swiper组件距离。由于导航点有默认交互区域，交互区域高度为32vp，所以无法让显示部分完全贴底。</p>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 10开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 936px;">     <h3 id="left" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">left<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="left" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>left(value: Length): T</p>     <p>导航点左侧相对于Swiper的位置。</p>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 10开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.43.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.43.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.43.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.43.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#length">Length</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>设置导航点左侧相对于Swiper的位置。</p>          <p>未设置left和right时，进行自适应大小布局，按照指示器本身大小和Swiper的大小在主轴方向上进行居中对齐。</p>          <p>设置为0时：按照0位置布局计算。</p>          <p>优先级：高于right属性。</p>          <p>取值范围：[0,Swiper宽度-导航点区域宽度]，超出该范围时，取最近的边界值。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div <h3 id="top" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">top<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" Length): T</p>     <p>导航点顶部相对于Swiper的位置。</p>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 10开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th <h3 id="bottom" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">bottom<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>bottom(value: Length): T</p>     <p>导航点底部相对于Swiper的位置。</p>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 10开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.46.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.46.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#length">Length</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>设置导航点底部相对于Swiper的位置。</p>          <p>未设置top和bottom时，进行自适应大小布局，按照指示器本身大小和Swiper的大小，在交叉轴方向上，位于底部，效果与设置bottom=0一致。</p>          <p>设置为0时：按照0位置布局计算。</p>          <p>优先级：低于top属性。</p>          <p>取值范围：[0,Swiper高度-导航点区域高度]，超出该范围时，取最近的边界值。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div <h3 id="bottom19" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">bottom<sup>19+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="bottom19" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>bottom(bottom: LengthMetrics | Length, ignoreSize: boolean): T</p>     <p>导航点底部相对于Swiper的位置，并可通过ignoreSize属性忽略导航点大小。</p>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 19开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 19开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.47.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.47.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.47.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.47.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">bottom</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkui-graphics#lengthmetrics12">LengthMetrics</a> | <a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#length">Length</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>设置导航点底部相对于Swiper的位置。</p>          <p>未设置top和bottom时，进行自适应大小布局，按照指示器本身大小和Swiper的大小，在交叉轴方向上，位于底部，效果与设置bottom=0一致。</p>          <p>设置为0时：按照0位置布局计算。</p>          <p>优先级：低于top属性。</p>          <p>取值范围：[0,Swiper高度-导航点区域高度]，超出该范围时，取最近的边界值。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">ignoreSize</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>设置是否忽略导航点本身大小，默认false。</p>          <p>设为true时可以将导航点更靠近Swiper底部，使用方法可以参考<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#示例9演示导航点space与bottom">示例9演示导航点space与bottom</a>。</p>          <p>说明：<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#digitindicator10">数字导航点</a>ignoreSize属性，不生效的场景如下：</p>          <p>• 当<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#vertical">vertical</a> 设置为false，且bottom &gt; 0。</p>          <p>• 当<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#vertical">vertical</a> 设置为true时：</p>          <p>1、bottom &gt; 0 时。</p>          <p>2、bottom设为undefined。</p>          <p>3、isSidebarMiddle设置为false时。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.60.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.60.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.60.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.60.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">maxDisplayCount</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>设置圆点导航点指示器样式下，导航点显示个数最大值，当实际导航点个数大于最大导航点个数时，会生效超长效果样式，样式如<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#示例5设置圆点导航点超长显示">示例5</a>所示。</p>          <p>默认值：这个属性没有默认值，如果设置异常值那等同于没有超长显示效果。</p>          <p>取值范围：[6, 9]</p>          <p><strong>说明：</strong></p>          <p>1、超长显示场景，目前暂时不支持交互功能（包括：手指点击拖拽、鼠标操作等）。</p>          <p>2、在超长显示场景下，中间页面对应的选中导航点的位置，并不是完全固定的，取决于之前的翻页操作序列。</p>          <p>3、当前仅支持displayCount为1的场景。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.61.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#dotindicator10">DotIndicator</a></td>         <td id="constructor-1" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">constructor<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>按压导航点时，导航点会放大至1.33倍显示，因此非按压态时导航点的可见范围边界至实际范围边界存在一定距离，该距离会随着itemWidth、itemHeight、selectedItemWidth、selectedItemHeight等参数变大而变大。</p>       <p>若页面数量较多、圆点导航点超出页面时，建议使用maxDisplayCount设置导航点显示个数。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 466px;">     <h2 id="digitindicator10" <p>设置箭头底板是否显示。为true时箭头底板显示，为false时箭头底板不显示。</p>          <p>默认值：false</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">isSidebarMiddle</td>         <td <p>默认值：24vp</p>          <p>在组件两侧显示：</p>          <p>默认值：32vp</p>          <p>不支持设置百分比。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">backgroundColor</td>         <td
