width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>设置底板颜色。</p>          <p>在导航点两侧显示：</p>          <p>默认值：'#00000000'</p>          <p>在组件两侧显示：</p>          <p>默认值：'#19182431'</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">arrowSize</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#length">Length</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>设置箭头大小。</p>          <p>在导航点两侧显示时：</p>          <p>默认值：18vp</p>          <p>在组件两侧显示时：</p>          <p>默认值：24vp</p>          <p><strong>说明：</strong></p>          <p>showBackground为true时，arrowSize为backgroundSize的3/4。</p>          <p>不支持设置百分比。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">arrowColor</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#resourcecolor">ResourceColor</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>设置箭头颜色。</p>          <p>默认值：'#182431'</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 477px;">     <h2 id="swiperautofill10" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">SwiperAutoFill<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link"     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 10开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.70.6.1.6.1.1" class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 573px;">     <h2 id="autoplayoptions18对象说明" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">AutoPlayOptions<sup>18+</sup>对象说明<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="autoplayoptions18对象说明" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 18开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.71.6.1.6.1.1" width="20%">名称</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.71.6.1.6.1.2"      <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>在按下事件中配置子组件是否立即停止播放。</p>          <p>设置为true时，停止播放。设置为false时，自动播放不中断。</p>          <p>默认值：true</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 182px;">     <h2 id="事件" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">事件<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="事件" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>除支持<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-component-general-events">通用事件</a>外，还支持以下事件：</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 649px;">     <h3 id="onchange" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">onChange<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="onchange" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>onChange(event: Callback&lt;number&gt;)</p>     <p>当前显示元素索引变化时触发该事件，返回值为当前显示元素的索引值。</p>     <p>Swiper组件结合LazyForEach使用时，不能在onChange事件里触发子页面UI的刷新。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <ul>        <li>如果是动画引起的索引变化，回调在动画结束时触发。</li>       </ul>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 10开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.73.10.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.73.10.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.73.10.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.73.10.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">event</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#callback12">Callback</a>&lt;number&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">当前显示元素的索引。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 813px;">     <h3 id="onanimationstart9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">onAnimationStart<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="onanimationstart9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>onAnimationStart(event: OnSwiperAnimationStartCallback)</p>     <p>切换动画开始时触发该回调。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <ul>        <li>调用此回调后，切换动画的逻辑将在渲染线程中执行，从而使处于空闲状态的主线程能够充分利用这段时间来加载子组件所需资源，减少后续在cachedCount范围内节点的预加载时间。最佳实践请参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/best-practices/bpta-swiper_high_performance_development_guide#section8783121513246" target="_blank">优化Swiper组件加载慢丢帧问题-提前加载数据</a>。</li>       </ul>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 10开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.74.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.74.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.74.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.74.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">event</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#onswiperanimationstartcallback18">OnSwiperAnimationStartCallback</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">切换动画开始时触发的回调。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <ul>        <li>当翻页动画时长为0时，只有以下场景会触发该回调：滑动翻页、自动轮播、调用SwiperController.showNext()和SwiperController.showPrevious()接口以及手指点击导航点翻页。</li>       </ul>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 713px;">     <h3 id="onanimationend9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">onAnimationEnd<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="onanimationend9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>onAnimationEnd(event: OnSwiperAnimationEndCallback)</p>     <p>切换动画结束时触发该回调。</p>     <p>当Swiper切换动效结束时触发，包括动画过程中手势中断，通过SwiperController调用finishAnimation。</p>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 10开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.75.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.75.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.75.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.75.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">event</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#onswiperanimationendcallback18">OnSwiperAnimationEndCallback</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">切换动画结束时触发的回调。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <ul>        <li>当翻页动画时长为0时，只有以下场景会触发该回调：滑动翻页、自动轮播、调用SwiperController.showNext()和SwiperController.showPrevious()接口以及手指点击导航点翻页。</li>       </ul>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 589px;">     <h3 id="ongestureswipe10" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">onGestureSwipe<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="ongestureswipe10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>onGestureSwipe(event: OnSwiperGestureSwipeCallback)</p>     <p>在页面跟手滑动过程中，逐帧触发该回调。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.76.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.76.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.76.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.76.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">event</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#onswipergestureswipecallback18">OnSwiperGestureSwipeCallback</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">在页面跟手滑动过程中，逐帧触发的回调。onGestureSwipe回调触发时机在onTouch之后，如果需要在离手后执行操作建议使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#onanimationstart9">onAnimationStart</a>。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 877px;">     <h3 id="customcontenttransition12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">customContentTransition<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="customcontenttransition12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>customContentTransition(transition: SwiperContentAnimatedTransition)</p>     <p>自定义Swiper页面切换动画。在页面跟手滑动和离手后执行切换动画的过程中，会对视窗内所有页面逐帧触发回调，开发者可以在回调中设置透明度、缩放比例、位移等属性来自定义切换动画。</p>     <p>使用说明：</p>     <p>1、循环场景下，设置prevMargin和nextMargin属性，使得Swiper前后端显示同一页面时，该接口不生效。</p>     <p>2、在页面跟手滑动和离手后执行切换动画的过程中，会对视窗内所有页面逐帧触发<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#swipercontenttransitionproxy12">SwiperContentTransitionProxy</a>回调。例如，当视窗内有下标为0、1的两个页面时，会每帧触发两次index值分别为0和1的回调。</p>     <p>3、设置displayCount属性的swipeByGroup参数为true时，若同组中至少有一个页面在视窗内时，则会对同组中所有页面触发回调，若同组所有页面均不在视窗内时，则会一起下渲染树。</p>     <p>4、在页面跟手滑动和离手后执行切换动画的过程中，默认动画（页面滑动）依然会发生，若希望页面不滑动，可以设置主轴方向上负的位移（translate属性）来抵消页面滑动。例如：当displayCount属性值为2，视窗内有下标为0、1的两个页面时，页面水平滑动过程中，可以逐帧设置第0页的translate属性在x轴上的值为-position * mainAxisLength来抵消第0页的位移，设置第1页的translate属性在x轴上的值为-(position - 1) * mainAxisLength来抵消第1页的位移。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.77.12.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.77.12.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.77.12.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.77.12.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">transition</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#swipercontentanimatedtransition12">SwiperContentAnimatedTransition</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Swiper自定义切换动画相关信息。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 709px;">     <h3 id="oncontentdidscroll12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">onContentDidScroll<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="oncontentdidscroll12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>onContentDidScroll(handler: ContentDidScrollCallback)</p>     <p>监听Swiper页面滑动事件。</p>     <p>使用说明：</p>     <p>1、循环场景下，设置prevMargin和nextMargin属性，使得Swiper前后端显示同一页面时，该接口不生效。</p>     <p>2、在页面滑动过程中，会对视窗内所有页面逐帧触发<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#contentdidscrollcallback12">ContentDidScrollCallback</a>回调。例如，当视窗内有下标为0、1的两个页面时，会每帧触发两次index值分别为0和1的回调。</p>     <p>3、设置displayCount属性的swipeByGroup参数为true时，若同组中至少有一个页面在视窗内时，则会对同组中所有页面触发回调。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.78.11.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.78.11.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.78.11.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.78.11.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">handler</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#contentdidscrollcallback12">ContentDidScrollCallback</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Swiper滑动时触发的回调。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 633px;">     <h3 id="onselected18" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">onSelected<sup>18+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>onSelected(event: Callback&lt;number&gt;)</p>     <p>当选中元素改变时触发该回调，返回值为当前选中的元素的索引值。</p>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 18开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 18开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p> width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">当前选中元素的索引。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>onSelected回调中不可修改swiper的index属性，不可调用SwiperController.changeIndex()、SwiperController.showNext()和SwiperController.showPrevious()方法。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 633px;">     <h3 id="onunselected18" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">onUnselected<sup>18+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" 18开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 18开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.80.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>onUnselected回调中不可修改swiper的index属性，不可调用SwiperController.changeIndex()、SwiperController.showNext()和SwiperController.showPrevious()方法。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 677px;">     <h3 id="oncontentwillscroll15" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">onContentWillScroll<sup>15+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="oncontentwillscroll15" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>onContentWillScroll(handler: ContentWillScrollCallback)</p>     <p>Swiper滑动行为拦截事件，在滑动前触发。Swiper会依据该事件的返回值来决定是否允许此次滑动行为。若返回true，表示允许此次滑动行为，Swiper页面将跟随滑动。若返回false，表示不允许此次滑动，页面将保持静止。</p>     <ol>      <li>       <p>触发该事件的场景仅限于手势操作，具体包括手指滑动、滚动鼠标滚轮以及使用键盘方向键进行焦点移动。</p></li>      <li>       <p>在手指滑动的过程中，每帧都将触发该事件，系统会依据事件的返回值判断是否对每帧的滑动做出响应。</p></li>      <li>       <p>对于滚动鼠标滚轮和使用键盘方向键进行焦点移动的场景，每次翻页操作都会触发一次该事件，翻页是否被允许将根据事件的返回值来决定。</p></li>     </ol>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 15开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 15开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.81.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.81.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.81.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.81.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">handler</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#contentwillscrollcallback15">ContentWillScrollCallback</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Swiper滑动时触发的回调。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 517px;"> tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="onscrollstatechanged20" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span <p>Swiper滑动状态变化事件回调，在跟手滑动、离手动画、停止三种滑动状态变化时触发，返回值为当前滑动状态。</p>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 20开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 20开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 708px;">     <h2 id="contentdidscrollcallback12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">ContentDidScrollCallback<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="contentdidscrollcallback12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span number) =&gt; void</p>     <p>Swiper滑动时触发的回调，参数可参考<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#swipercontenttransitionproxy12">SwiperContentTransitionProxy</a>中的说明。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder"> device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">ContentWillScrollCallback<sup>15+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>type ContentWillScrollCallback = (result: SwiperContentWillScrollResult) =&gt; boolean</p>     <p>Swiper即将滑动前触发的回调，返回值表示是否允许此次滑动。</p>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 15开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 15开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left"   <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">result</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">即将滑动的相关信息，主要包括：当前页面对应的index、滑动方向上即将显示的页面index和此次滑动的位移。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Swiper是否响应本次滑动，true表示响应，false表示不响应。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection"     <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span   <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 15开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 15开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>    <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>此次滑动的位移，带有符号，正负分别指示不同的翻页方向。正数表示从index=1向index=0翻页，负数表示从index=0向index=1翻页。</p>          <p>在手指滑动的场景中，该值为滑动事件中每帧传递下来的偏移量。在滚动鼠标滚轮和使用键盘方向键导航的场景中，该值代表即将翻页的距离。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 711px;">     <h2 id="swiperanimationevent10对象说明" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 834px;">     <h2 id="swipercontentanimatedtransition12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">SwiperContentAnimatedTransition<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="swipercontentanimatedtransition12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>Swiper自定义切换动画相关信息。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.90.5.1.6.1.1" width="20%">名称</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.90.5.1.6.1.2" width="20%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.90.5.1.6.1.3" width="20%">只读</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.90.5.1.6.1.4" width="20%">可选</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.90.5.1.6.1.5" width="20%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">timeout</td>         <td width="20%">Swiper自定义切换动画超时时间。从页面执行默认动画（页面滑动）至移出视窗外的第一帧开始计时，如果到达该时间后，开发者仍未调用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#swipercontenttransitionproxy12">SwiperContentTransitionProxy</a>的finishTransition接口通知Swiper组件此页面的自定义动画已结束，那么组件就会认为此页面的自定义动画已结束，立即将该页面节点下渲染树。单位ms，默认值为0。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">transition</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">Callback&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#swipercontenttransitionproxy12">SwiperContentTransitionProxy</a>&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">自定义切换动画具体内容。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 302px;">     <h2 id="swipercontenttransitionproxy12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">SwiperContentTransitionProxy<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="swipercontenttransitionproxy12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>Swiper自定义切换动画执行过程中，返回给开发者的proxy对象。开发者可通过该对象获取自定义动画视窗内的页面信息，同时，也可以通过调用该对象的finishTransition接口通知Swiper组件页面自定义动画已结束。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 714px;">     <h3 id="属性-1" class="firsth2">属性<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="属性-1" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.92.2.1.6.1.1" width="20%">名称</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.92.2.1.6.1.2" width="20%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.92.2.1.6.1.3" width="20%">只读</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.92.2.1.6.1.4" width="20%">可选</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.92.2.1.6.1.5" width="20%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">selectedIndex</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">当前选中页面的索引。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">index</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">视窗内页面的索引。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">position</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">index页面相对于Swiper主轴起始位置（selectedIndex对应页面的起始位置）的移动比例。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">mainAxisLength</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">index对应页面在主轴方向上的长度，单位vp。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <ul>        <li>         <p>例如，当前选中的子组件的索引为0，从第0页切换到第1页的动画过程中，每帧都会对视窗内所有页面触发回调，当视窗内有第0页和第1页两页时，每帧会触发两次回调。其中，第一次回调的selectedIndex为0、index为0、position为当前帧第0页相对于动画开始前第0页的移动比例，mainAxisLength为主轴方向上第0页的长度。第二次回调的selectedIndex仍为0、index为1、position为当前帧第1页相对于动画开始前第0页的移动比例，mainAxisLength为主轴方向上第1页的长度。</p></li>        <li>         <p>若动画曲线为弹簧插值曲线，从第0页切换到第1页的动画过程中，可能会因为离手时的位置和速度，先过滑到第2页，再回弹到第1页，该过程中每帧会对视窗内第1页和第2页触发回调。</p></li>       </ul>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 318px;">     <h3 id="finishtransition12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">finishTransition<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="finishtransition12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>finishTransition(): void</p>     <p>通知Swiper组件，此页面的自定义动画已结束。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 513px;">     <h3 id="indicatorstyledeprecated" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">indicatorStyle<sup>(deprecated)</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="indicatorstyledeprecated" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>indicatorStyle(value?: IndicatorStyle)</p>     <p>设置导航点样式。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从API version 8开始支持，从API version 10开始废弃，建议使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper#indicator10">indicator</a>替代。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.94.7.1.5.1.1" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 146px;">     <h2 id="示例" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">示例<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i
